thing: an entity that can be referred to and counted as one, treated as having some kind of identity and properties. A thing can be an object, abstractum or occurrence. An object is a thing that is physical, tangible and persists in time, bear properties and stand in relations. An abstractum is a thing that is identified by their role in thought, meaning or content; it exists in mind as ideas, qualities or concepts rather than as a physical and tangible object. An occurrence is an event or process in happening and unfolding through time.
